### [1] [TBD LBD: The nature of `little blue dots'](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12509)
*Albert Sneppen,Darach Watson,James H. Matthews,Georgios Nikopoulos*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文提出LBDs（little blue dots）是LRDs（little red dots）在较低柱密度下的对应体，属于同一气体茧状AGN演化序列的不同阶段；通过Sirocco辐射转移模型分析，揭示了柱密度增加如何系统性地改变光谱特征（如Balmer跳变、X射线减弱、指数型谱线翼等），并用三个LBD观测样本验证了Balmer跳变的存在。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解释新发现的little blue dots（LBDs）的物理本质，并将其与先前模型预测及已知的little red dots（LRDs）建立联系。

Method: 基于Sirocco辐射转移模型，系统模拟不同氢柱密度（N_H）下气体茧状AGN的光谱特征，分析Balmer连续谱吸收/发射、X射线衰减、谱线轮廓等随柱密度的变化规律，并与观测到的LBD光谱进行比对。

Result: 发现柱密度约few×10^24 cm⁻²时出现Balmer跳变和X射线弱化但无强Balmer吸收的LBD类光谱；更高柱密度则过渡为LRD类Balmer-break光谱；电子散射主导谱线指数翼和X射线抑制；三个LBD样本中确认存在Balmer跳变。

Conclusion: LBDs是低柱密度端的气体茧状AGN，与LRDs构成同一演化序列的不同相位；该框架统一解释了其光谱共性（Balmer跳变、X射线弱、He II发射、窄Hα线等），并为理解 obscured AGN的遮蔽结构提供新视角。

Abstract: Previous Sirocco radiative-transfer models of gas-cocooned AGN predicted lower-column counterparts to little red dots (LRDs): compact, X-ray-weak sources with bluer continuum slopes and Balmer jumps rather than Balmer breaks. The recently identified population of little blue dots (LBDs) closely resembles this predicted phase. Here we explore these lower-column-density cocoons in which nebular recombination emission remains visible while strong Balmer-continuum absorption is avoided. We find that a sequence of increasing column density connects more classical AGN spectra, Balmer-jump LBD-like spectra at $N_{\rm H}\!\sim\!{\rm few}\times10^{24} \mathrm{cm^{-2}}$, and Balmer-break LRD-like spectra at higher columns. In this sequence, electron scattering produces exponential line wings and suppresses X-ray emission before strong Balmer absorption features, characteristic of higher column densities, appear. We therefore propose that LBDs are lower-column analogues of LRDs within a common gas-cocooned AGN sequence. This interpretation predicts that Balmer-jump emission, X-ray weakness, permitted lines with exponential wings, He II $λ$4686 emission, smaller H$α$ FWHM values and equivalent widths than in LRDs, and weak or absent absorption features are characteristic of LBDs. We compare to three example LBD spectra and identify Balmer-jump signatures in them.

</details>


### [2] [Unification models of Active Galactic Nuclei](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12511)
*Claudio Ricci*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本章综述了活动星系核（AGN）的统一模型，涵盖其物理结构、分类方案与演化过程，并重点讨论基于取向的传统模型、辐射调控模型、演化因素（如星系并合、宿主星系性质、红移趋势）以及挑战传统框架的变脸AGN。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解AGN观测多样性的物理起源，调和不同观测类型之间的关系，并解释变脸AGN等异常现象对传统统一模型的挑战。

Method: 文献综述与理论模型分析，整合观测证据与物理机制（如取向效应、辐射反馈、星系演化）。

Result: 系统梳理了AGN统一模型的发展脉络，强调覆盖因子、辐射反馈及演化效应的关键作用，并指出变脸AGN揭示了统一框架需纳入时变物理过程。

Conclusion: AGN统一模型正从静态取向主导转向动态、多物理机制耦合的框架，需综合取向、辐射反馈与演化历史以全面解释观测多样性。

Abstract: This chapter presents an overview of the unification models for Active Galactic Nuclei (AGN), focusing on the physical structures, classification schemes, and evolutionary processes that characterize accreting supermassive black holes. We introduce the fundamental components of AGN, including the supermassive black hole, accretion disk, jets, outflows, broad-line and narrow-line regions, polar dust and the dusty anisotropic obscurer. The traditional orientation-based unification model is reviewed, with a focus on the role of the covering factor of the obscuring material in shaping observed properties. We introduce the radiation-regulated unification model, which accounts for the influence of radiative feedback on the nuclear environment of SMBHs. We also examine the evolutionary aspects of AGN unification, including the impact of galaxy mergers, host galaxy properties, and redshift-dependent trends. Finally, we discuss changing-look AGN, which challenge conventional unification frameworks by exhibiting dramatic spectral variability.

</details>


### [3] [Bar-induced migration of $ω$ Centauri away from Gaia Sausage-Enceladus](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12516)
*Adam M. Dillamore,Hanyuan Zhang,Vasily Belokurov*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文探讨了球状星团ω Cen是否起源于银河系的Gaia Sausage-Enceladus（GSE）并合事件，并通过数值模拟研究其轨道演化是否可由银河系棒状结构扰动解释；结果表明该起源在动力学和化学上是可能的，但需较低的棒模式速度（Ω_b ≲ 26 km s⁻¹ kpc⁻¹），与当前主流估计不符。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: ω Cen被怀疑起源于GSE并合事件，但其当前轨道与GSE碎片显著不同，因此需探究其是否通过银河系棒扰动迁移至当前位置。

Method: 在包含减速棒的现实银河系势场中，对GSE碎片和ω Cen进行数值轨道模拟，并分析其在(L_z, E)相空间中的化学丰度分布（[α/M]）及回溯轨道。

Result: 模拟显示ω Cen可回溯至GSE碎片所占相空间区域，但要求棒模式速度Ω_b ≲ 26 km s⁻¹ kpc⁻¹，显著低于近期多数估计值。

Conclusion: ω Cen起源于GSE在动力学和化学上是可行的，但需重新评估当前关于银河系棒模式速度的共识。

Abstract: The globular cluster $ω$ Cen has been suggested to have originated in the Gaia Sausage-Enceladus (GSE) merger event, possibly as its nuclear star cluster. However, the present-day orbits of $ω$ Cen and the GSE debris are very different. We investigate the scenario in which $ω$ Cen originated in the GSE and migrated to its current position due to perturbations from the Galactic bar. The [$α$/M] distributions of stars located between the GSE debris and $ω$ Cen in $(L_z,E)$ space tentatively support this scenario, but are not conclusive. We run simulations of the GSE debris and $ω$ Cen in a realistic Milky Way potential with a decelerating bar at various present-day pattern speeds. We find that $ω$ Cen can indeed be traced back to the phase space region occupied by the GSE debris. However, this likely requires a pattern speed of $Ω_\mathrm{b}\lesssim26$ km s$^{-1}$ kpc$^{-1}$, which is much lower than most recent estimates. We conclude that a GSE origin for $ω$ Cen is dynamically and chemically plausible, but this would require a re-evaluation of the current consensus on the bar's pattern speed.

</details>


### [4] [The Hubble Missing Globular Clusters Survey IV. Ultra-faint compact satellites of the Milky Way. The case of Koposov 2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12517)
*M. Bellazzini,R. Pascale,E. Dodd,E. Ceccarelli,D. Massari,M. Libralato,S. Cassisi,M. De Leo,A. Della Croce,E. Vesperini,A. Mucciarelli,E. Dalessandro,M. Salaris,F. Aguado-Agelet,A. Bellini,F. R. Ferraro,B. Lanzoni,M. Monelli,S. Saracino*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文利用哈勃太空望远镜（HST）深测光数据与光谱金属丰度，对极微弱致密天体Koposov 2进行贝叶斯等龄线拟合，精确测定其距离（23.4±0.6 kpc）、年龄（13.7^{+0.9}_{-1.3} Gyr）、半光半径（2.7 pc）、总光度（M_V = −0.95）和恒星质量（372 M⊙），确认其为银河系中已知最贫金属的束缚星团而非矮星系，并指出多数UFCS在M_V–R_h图中与银河系疏散星团位置重叠，暗示可能的新形成通道。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Ultra Faint Compact Satellites (UFCS) 在光度–半光半径图（M_V–R_h）中位于矮星系与球状星团的重叠区，加之其极暗、遥远，其本质（星团还是矮星系）长期不确定；Koposov 2作为其中最贫金属的候选体，亟需高精度测距与定年以判别其性质。

Method: 结合Missing Globular Clusters Survey（MGCS）的HST深测光数据与光谱金属丰度，采用光谱约束的贝叶斯等龄线拟合方法测定距离与年龄；通过完备性校正的光度函数拟合推断初始质量函数斜率；建模表面恒星密度场以获得半光半径、总光度和恒星质量；并对比UFCS在M_V–R_h平面上的整体分布。

Result: Koposov 2的距离为23.4±0.6 kpc，年龄为13.7^{+0.9}_{-1.3} Gyr（与最老球状星团相当），半光半径仅2.7 pc，总光度M_V=−0.95，恒星质量约372 M⊙；其光度函数显示低质量端显著缺失（x=−0.35）；其结构参数明显偏离矮星系，更接近致密星团；多数UFCS落在疏散星团所在的M_V–R_h区域。

Conclusion: Koposov 2本质上是一个古老、致密、严重质量亏损的球状星团，而非矮星系；UFCS整体可能包含一类新型致密星团，其形成或演化路径不同于经典球状星团，部分或起源于类似疏散星团的环境。

Abstract: In the last decades a number of extremely faint and compact Galactic satellites (Ultra Faint Compact Satellites; UFCS) have been discovered by large panoramic surveys. Their nature is uncertain due to their location in the overlapping dwarf galaxy-star cluster region of the $M_V-R_h$ plane and their faintness and distance. Here we show how the deep HST photometry from the Missing Globular Clusters Survey (MGCS), combined with spectroscopic metallicities, provides new insight into the nature of these satellites through accurate distance and age estimates. We consider the case of Koposov 2, currently the most metal-poor bound star cluster known in the entire Milky Way or an extreme case of Ultra Faint Dwarf galaxy. By performing a spectroscopically-informed bayesian isochrone fit on the MGCS data we find $(m-M)_0=16.85\pm 0.06$ ($D=23.4\pm 0.6$ kpc) and age=$13.7^{+0.9}_{-1.3}$ Gyr, showing that, contrary to previous age estimates, Koposov 2 is as old as the oldest Galactic globular clusters. The luminosity function, corrected for incompleteness, is well reproduced by a model with the same age and metallicity and a slope of the mass function $x=-0.35$, suggesting a significant depletion of faint stars. We model the surface stellar density field, deriving new robust estimates of the half-light radius ($R_h=0.39^{+0.06}_{-0.04}$ arcsec, corresponding to $R_h=2.7^{+0.4}_{-0.3}$ pc), of the absolute integrated magnitude ($M_V=-0.95\pm0.22$) and of the stellar mass ($M_{\star}=371.8\pm41.6M_{\odot}$), showing that Koposov 2 is much more compact than dwarf galaxies of similar stellar mass. The new evidence significantly support the hypothesis that Koposov 2 is a star cluster that may have lost a large fraction of its original mass. Finally we show that most UFCS lie in the same locus of the $M_V - R_h$ plane as Galactic open clusters, hinting to a possible additional channel for their formation.

</details>


### [5] [Dark and Luminous Matter in the Coma Cluster: Probing Galaxy Cluster Assembly Through Filaments with Weak Lensing and Multiwavelength Observations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12523)
*K. HyeongHan,K. Finner,M. James Jee,W. Lee,Y. Jiménez-Teja,S. Cha,W. Kang,H. S. Hwang,H. Cho,E. Churazov,I. Khabibullin,N. Lyskova,R. Sunyaev,A. M. Bykov*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文利用Subaru/Hyper Suprime-Cam对后发座星系团（Coma cluster）开展宽视场弱引力透镜分析，结合X射线、射电与光学观测，揭示其暗物质分布、子结构及与星系际介质和星系际纤维（ICFs）的关联；结果支持一个主-次并合（~1:8）图像，并发现ICFs区域暗物质主导性更强。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 后发座星系团是研究宇宙网中星系团组装的关键实验室，需通过多波段联合观测厘清其暗物质分布、子结构及与星系、热气体和星系际纤维（ICFs）的关系。

Method: 基于Subaru/Hyper Suprime-Cam宽场（~12 deg²）弱引力透镜数据重建二维质量分布；拟合单/双NFW晕模型；计算孔径质量密度剖面；并与eROSITA X射线、光学光谱、射电及气体分数诊断结果交叉比对。

Result: 单晕NFW拟合得M₂₀₀c = 8.2±0.7×10¹⁴ M⊙；双晕拟合给出主晕（NGC 4874）与次晕（NGC 4839）质量比约1:8；WL与X射线表面亮度在ICFs方向（110°和340°）相关最强；ICFs区域M/Lᵣ达~1000 M⊙/L⊙，显著高于整体平均值（250±66 M⊙/L⊙）。

Conclusion: 联合弱透镜与多波段观测可有效刻画星系团组装历史，并证实星系际纤维中存在显著暗物质成分，支持其作为正在吸积的低光度暗物质结构。

Abstract: The Coma cluster (Abell 1656; $z=0.023$) is a nearby rich galaxy cluster and a key laboratory for studying cluster assembly in the Cosmic Web. We characterize its projected dark matter distribution and connection to galaxies, the intracluster medium, and reported intracluster filaments (ICFs) with wide-field ($\sim$12-deg$^2$) Subaru/Hyper Suprime-Cam weak-lensing (WL) analysis. We reconstruct the two-dimensional mass distribution, fit Navarro-Frenk-White (NFW) models, derive an aperture mass densitometry profile, and compare the WL signal with optical spectroscopy, eROSITA X-ray observations, radio data, and gas fraction diagnostics. A single-halo NFW fit yields $M_{200\mathrm{c}}=8.2\pm0.7\times10^{14}~M_{\odot}$. The aperture mass profile agrees with the best-fit NFW model and the X-ray hydrostatic mass at $R\gtrsim20'$ ($\sim$560 kpc), suggesting little merger-induced bias in the global WL mass, while the inner region shows substantial hydrostatic bias. A two-halo NFW fit centered on NGC 4874 and NGC 4839 gives masses of $7.8\pm0.6$ and $0.9\pm0.2\times10^{14}~M_{\odot}$, implying a $\sim$1:8 minor merger. The gas mass fraction suggests that the system is returning from first apocenter. We find a positive spatial correlation between the WL signal and X-ray surface brightness, strongest along the ICF directions ($110^{\circ}$ and $340^{\circ}$), where shear-selected subhalos are predominantly detected. The Coma $r$-band mass-to-light ratio is radially constant with $\langle M/L_r\rangle\simeq250\pm66~M_{\odot}/L_{\odot}$ within $R_{200\mathrm{c}}$, whereas the northern and western ICFs show higher values of $\sim1000~M_{\odot}/L_{\odot}$, suggesting stronger dark matter dominance. These results show that joint WL and multiwavelength analyses can effectively probe cluster assembly and the dark matter content of ICFs.

</details>


### [6] [Getting to know the Stellar Clusters in NGC 1569: Bayesian inference of stellar cluster properties in a dwarf starburst galaxy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12536)
*Bjarki Björgvinsson,Anna F. McLeod,Bronwyn Reichardt Chu,Magdalena J. Hamel-Bravo,Deanne B. Fisher,Mark R. Krumholz*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文利用哈勃太空望远镜成像与凯克宇宙网络成像仪光谱数据，结合贝叶斯建模（考虑IMF随机采样不确定性），推断NGC 1569星团的质量与年龄，并探讨其与局部星际介质条件（如金属丰度、电离态、密度）的相关性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解矮星暴星系NGC 1569中星团形成如何受局部星际介质条件影响，并评估多波段观测（尤其UV与NIR）对打破星团年龄-质量简并的作用。

Method: 基于HST高分辨率成像与KCWI积分场光谱，采用前向建模的贝叶斯方法推断星团质量与年龄，充分考虑初始质量函数（IMF）随机采样的不确定性；通过不同滤光组合（含模拟UV/NIR扩展）检验光度覆盖对参数约束的影响。

Result: 现有数据已能较好约束星团参数；加入UV/NIR可进一步缓解年龄-质量简并；发现星团截断质量随银心距变化（反映ISM密度依赖）、星团质量正相关于金属丰度与气体电离态。

Conclusion: IMF感知的贝叶斯建模能有效解析邻近星暴矮星系中的星团种群，揭示星团形成与反馈过程对局域星系环境的敏感依赖性。

Abstract: We present a Bayesian analysis of star clusters in the dwarf starburst galaxy NGC 1569 based on high-resolution Hubble Space Telescope imaging combined with integral-field spectroscopy from the Keck Cosmic Web Imager, obtained as part of the DUVET survey. For each cluster identified, we infer posterior probability distributions for mass and age using a forward modelling method that properly accounts for uncertainties due to stochastic sampling of the IMF. We investigate how the inferred properties depend on photometric coverage by repeating the analysis with different filter combinations, including mock extensions to the ultraviolet and near-infrared that emulate the addition of HST UV bands and James Webb Space Telescope imaging. We find that, while inclusion of these wavelength regimes further breaks age and mass degeneracies, the currently available data yields reasonably strong constraints on cluster parameters. We compare inferred cluster properties to the conditions of the local interstellar medium, and find evidence for multiple interesting correlations. The truncation mass of the cluster mass function varies with galactocentric distance, particularly moving off the disk, consistent with a dependence on the density of the interstellar medium. Cluster mass positively correlates with metallicity, suggesting that massive clusters preferentially form in pre-enriched gas, and the ionisation state of the gas, reflecting the increased prevalence of high-mass stars in high-mass clusters. These results demonstrate the power of Bayesian, initial mass function-aware modelling for resolving cluster populations in nearby starburst dwarfs and provide new insight into how cluster formation and feedback respond to local galactic conditions.

</details>


### [7] [DESI as sparse Integral Field Spectrograph I: Spatially resolved chemical enrichment in star-forming galaxies at $z\leq0.1$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12541)
*Vibhore Negi,Ravi Joshi,B. Vishnupriya,Xue-Bing Wu,Hassen M. Yesuf,Luis C. Ho,Ayan Acharyya,Ramya Sethuram,Abhijeet Anand,Michele Fumagalli,Celine Peroux*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本研究利用DESI多光纤光谱数据，对2291个z≤0.1的恒星形成星系进行了空间分辨的气体金属丰度分析，发现金属丰度梯度随恒星质量、星系尺寸和恒星年龄分布系统性变化，揭示了恒星形成效率、恒星反馈与金属贫乏气体吸积在星系化学结构演化中的协同作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解星系中径向化学丰度结构的物理起源，特别是金属丰度梯度如何受恒星质量、星系尺寸、恒星年龄分布及气体吸积等过程影响。

Method: 基于DESI多光纤光谱数据，将其作为稀疏积分场光谱仪使用，对2291个z≤0.1的恒星形成星系进行空间分辨的气体相金属丰度（O/H）测量，分析其径向金属丰度梯度、与恒星质量/尺寸/年龄的关系。

Result: 1）大质量星系内区（<2Re）金属丰度梯度陡峭（~−0.08 dex/Re），矮星系则近似平坦（~−0.02 dex/Re）；2）在大半径（~5Re）处金属丰度轮廓变平，且该平坦值跨质量范围一致；3）金属丰度梯度–恒星质量关系在log(M⋆/M⊙)≈10.5处发生转折；4）相同质量下，致密星系比延展星系梯度更平、中心丰度更高；5）外围恒星越年轻，梯度越陡，支持由内向外的盘演化模型。

Conclusion: 星系径向化学结构由恒星形成效率、恒星反馈（如外流）与金属贫乏原初气体吸积共同调控；金属梯度转折和外围平坦化暗示高质星系趋于化学平衡，而低质星系受持续吸积主导。

Abstract: We present a spatially resolved chemical abundance analysis of 2291 star-forming galaxies at $z \leq 0.1$, spanning nearly four orders of magnitude in stellar mass ($8 \le \rm log (M_{\star}/M_{\odot}) \le 11.5$), by exploiting the multi-fibre spectra from the Dark Energy Spectroscopic Instrument (DESI) as a sparse integral field spectrograph. In the inner regions ($<2R_e$), the radial gas-phase metallicity profiles show an outward-declining trend for massive galaxies, with the steepest gradient ($\nabla_{log(O/H)}$) $\sim-0.08$ dex/R$_{e}$, whereas low-mass dwarf galaxies exhibit nearly flat profiles ($\nabla_{log(O/H)}\sim-0.02$ dex/R$_{e}$). The large galactocentric radii ($\sim$5 R$_{e}$) probed in this study, reveal flat metallicity profiles near the disk-halo interface. Strikingly, these flat metallicity values are consistent across a wide stellar mass range, likely reflecting the influence of low SFR and metal poor inflows in the outer regions. The metallicity gradient - stellar mass relation exhibits a turnover at $\log(M_\star/M_\odot) \sim 10.5$, beyond which gradients become shallower, possibly driven by the chemical equilibrium in the inner disk of massive galaxies and/or dilution from cosmic gas accretion. At fixed stellar mass, a strong size dependence is observed, where compact galaxies show flatter gradients and higher central enrichment than their extended counterparts. The abundance gradients are further linked with the stellar age distribution within the galactic disk, where galaxies with younger outskirts show steeper gradients than the ones with older outskirts, consistent with ongoing inside-out disc growth sustaining centrally concentrated chemical enrichment. These results underscore the interplay of star formation efficiency, stellar feedback, and metal-poor gas accretion in governing the radial chemical structure in galaxies.

</details>


### [8] [Constraining the Geometry of Galactic Dark Matter with Gaia Data Release 3](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12548)
*Francesco Sylos Labini,Roberto Capuzzo-Dolcetta*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文利用Gaia DR3数据，精确测量银河系中垂直高度z和银心距离R范围内的旋转曲线vc(R,z)与垂直加速度az(R,z)，发现球形暗物质晕模型无法解释观测到的vc和az随高度变化的特征，而盘状暗物质分布模型则与数据高度吻合，从而强烈支持暗物质呈盘状分布而非球形晕。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 通过高精度观测约束银河系暗物质分布的几何形态，特别是检验球形暗物质晕与盘状暗物质分布哪种更符合观测。

Method: 基于Gaia DR3数据，在z∈(-2,2) kpc、R∈(8.5,14) kpc范围内提取高精度（误差<5%）的旋转曲线vc(R,z)和垂直加速度az(R,z)，并对比不同暗物质分布模型（球形晕 vs. 盘状分布）对观测量的理论预测。

Result: 球形暗物质晕（rs∼15 kpc）对内盘区域vc(R,z)和az(R,z)贡献极小，无法再现观测到的高度依赖性；而盘状暗物质分布能显著改善拟合，与数据高度一致。

Conclusion: 观测强烈支持银河系暗物质呈盘状分布，而非传统球形晕模型；未来Gaia数据将进一步严格检验暗物质的几何与空间分布。

Abstract: We derive both the mid-plane and off-plane rotation curves, $v_c(R,z)$, and the vertical acceleration, $a_z(R,z)$, of the Milky Way (MW) using \textit{Gaia}~DR3 data over the ranges of vertical heights $z \in (-2,2)\,$ kpc and galactocentric distances $R \in (8.5,14)$ kpc where the velocity components are determined with high precision, i.e., with an error $< 5\%$. In contrast, the vertical acceleration $a_z(R,z)$ is dominated by model-dependent systematics, with uncertainties of up to $\sim 20\%$. This level of accuracy allows us to place stringent constraints on the geometry of the MW's dark matter (DM) distribution, as the vertical gradients of the gravitational potential attain their maximum within this range of radial and vertical distances corresponding to the characteristic scales of the disk. We find that models including the observed stellar components together with a spherical DM halo fail to reproduce both the pronounced variation of $v_c(R,z)$ with height and the observed behavior of $a_z(R,z)$. In particular, spherical halos with a scale radius of $r_s \sim 15$ kpc contribute negligibly to the off-plane rotation curve and vertical acceleration in the inner disk, leaving these features primarily determined by the stellar mass distribution. Conversely, models in which DM is confined to a flattened, disk-like configuration predict substantial contributions to both $v_c(R,z)$ and $a_z(R,z)$, resulting in a markedly better agreement with the data. We conclude that disk-like DM distributions are strongly favored over spherical halo models. Forthcoming Gaia data releases will enable even more stringent tests of the geometry and distribution of the MW's DM component.

</details>


### [9] [CAPOS: The bulge Cluster APOgee Survey XII. Abundances for 98 PIGS metal-poor Bulge field giants](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12583)
*Carolina Salgado,Sandro Villanova,Doug Geisler,Nicolás Barrera*

TL;DR: 本文通过化学-动力学联合方法，利用APOGEE数据和轨道积分，识别出98颗动力学定义的金属贫乏核球场星，并分析其α元素与Fe峰元素丰度，揭示其原位形成并受棒演化影响的起源。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 确认98颗核球成员星，[Fe/H]分布为−2.5至−0.4（中位数−1.71），高于内晕（中位数−1.96）；呈现高α序列，[Si/Fe]与[Mg/Fe]随[Fe/H]轻微下降，[Ni/Fe]≈0，[Mn/Fe]随[Fe/H]下降并在高金属量处微升；未发现显著的[Si/Fe]径向或垂向梯度。

Abstract: The inner Milky Way hosts overlapping stellar populations (bar--bulge, inner thin and thick disks, and halo), complicating population assignments along the line of sight. A joint chemical--dynamical approach is required to isolate a clean field bulge sample. Metal-poor bulge stars are valuable as they likely trace the earliest phases of chemical enrichment in the inner Galaxy. We aim to characterize the alpha-element (Si, Mg) and selected Fe-peak abundances of a dynamically defined sample of bulge field stars, and to contrast these trends with the inner-halo tail in the metal-poor regime. We analyze metal-poor candidates from the Pristine Inner Galaxy Survey observed by the bulge Cluster APOGEE Survey. Using APOGEE/ASPCAP abundances (S/N >= 50), we integrate full 6D orbits in a barred Milky Way potential. Bulge membership is defined via orbital confinement using an apocenter cut and the high-density locus in the (E_J, L_z) plane, with uncertainties estimated using Monte Carlo simulations. We identify 98 stars as bulge members. The metallicity distribution spans -2.5 <= [Fe/H] <= -0.4, with a median [Fe/H] = -1.71, offset to higher metallicity than the inner halo (median [Fe/H] = -1.96). The sample follows a high-alpha sequence with slopes d[Si/Fe]/d[Fe/H] = -0.020(+0.012,-0.051) and d[Mg/Fe]/d[Fe/H] = -0.097(+0.062,-0.133). Fe-peak tracers show [Ni/Fe] ~ 0, while [Mn/Fe] declines with [Fe/H] with a mild upturn at higher metallicity. We detect no significant [Si/Fe] gradients with R_apo or Z_max (+0.010(+0.018,0.000) and +0.006(+0.022,-0.011) dex kpc^-1, respectively). Results are insensitive to Omega_p, yielding indistinguishable memberships. The chemo-orbital evidence favors an in situ origin within the inner Galaxy for the metal-poor bulge field, enriched at early times and rearranged by secular bar evolution, with a minor contribution from halo stars at the most metal-poor end.

### [10] [Influence of the resonance ring gravity on the stellar velocity distribution near the OLR of the Galactic bar](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12589)
*A. M. Melnik,E. N. Podzolkova*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文构建了一个包含棒、核球、盘和晕的银河系二维模型，研究了椭圆共振环（R1、R2 和 r）对引力扰动的影响，并验证了其解析表达式的精度；结果表明这些环的引力对棒外林达布拉德共振（OLR）附近的表观圆周运动调整影响甚微。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建含解析棒、核球、盘和晕的二维银河系模型；基于环结构推导径向和方位角方向的引力扰动解析表达式（以多项式形式表示F_R，再导出F_T）；通过数值微分势函数与解析结果对比验证精度。

Result: F_R和F_T的解析计算与数值微分结果偏差分别不超过5.7%和1.3%；椭圆环引力对OLR附近表观圆周运动调整影响很小。

Conclusion: 椭圆共振环的引力扰动可用高精度解析公式描述，但其对OLR区域动力学演化的作用可忽略。

Abstract: We constructed the 2D model of the Galaxy which initially includes an analytical bar, bulge, disk and halo. The model disk forms the outer elliptical resonance rings R1 and R2 located near the outer Lindblad resonance of the bar (OLR), as well as the inner resonance ring r located near the corotation radius (CR). As the density of stars in the elliptical rings increased, we introduced additional gravitational perturbations created by the rings. The radial component of gravitational perturbations from the elliptical rings, F_R, at a point with the Galactocentric coordinates (R, theta) was represented as a combination of three polynomials in powers R/Re or Re/R, where Re is the distance to the midline (middle) of the ring at a given angle theta. The azimuthal component of the disturbances, F_T, was calculated using the force F_R. The difference between the values of the force F_R (F_T) calculated using the numerical differentiation of the potential and using the analytical representation does not exceed 5.7% (1.3%) of the maximum value of the force F_R generated by the elliptical rings. In general, the gravity of the elliptical rings has little effect on the process of adjustment of epicyclic motions near the OLR of the bar.

### [11] [Feedback-Free Star Formation in Clusters within a Galaxy Simulated at High Resolution in Cosmic Dawn](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12605)
*Hou-Zun Chen,Zhaozhou Li,Avishai Dekel,Zhiyuan Yao,Nir Mandelker,Xi Kang*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文通过高分辨率宇宙学模拟，揭示了早期宇宙中大质量星系内反馈自由星暴（FFB）的形成机制，成功再现了JWST观测到的超亮星系，并解释了球状星团可能的起源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解释詹姆斯·韦布太空望远镜（JWST）观测到的高红移（z~10）超亮星系的形成机制，并探究早期星团（尤其是球状星团前身）的诞生条件与演化路径。

Method: 采用GIZMO代码进行宇宙学zoom-in模拟，空间分辨率达≤3 pc，引入3.4 Myr超新星反馈延迟，以捕捉无反馈主导的星暴过程（FFB）；分析恒星形成效率、星团质量函数、金属丰度、反馈外流及动力学演化等物理量。

Result: 模拟成功再现FFB模型预测和JWST观测；发现z~10时冷气体流持续供能，星系致密（Re~1 kpc），密度超过FFB阈值；90%恒星在星团中形成，其中<10^7 M⊙星团以<3 Myr短时爆发为主（局地SFE≈0.5）；识别出>10^5个大质量星团，质量分布近似幂律（dN/dlogM ∝ M^{-1.06}）；中心1 kpc内星团快速并合形成核星团；反馈外流温度~10^7 K、速度~2000 km/s；金属丰度范围-2.01 < log(Z/Z⊙) < -0.45，表明快速重循环。

Conclusion: 早期高密度环境下的反馈自由星暴是形成超亮星系和大量致密星团的关键机制；这些星团多数经历剧烈动力学演化，部分可能幸存为低红移球状星团，为理解GCs的起源提供了关键数值证据。

Abstract: We perform a cosmological zoom-in simulation of a massive galaxy ($M_s\sim10^{10}\rm M_\odot$ at $z\sim10$) using the GIZMO code. By employing $\leq 3\rm pc$ resolution and a $3.4\rm Myr$ supernova feedback delay, we capture the feedback-free starbursts (FFB) in clusters. The simulation reproduces FFB model predictions and super-bright galaxies observed by JWST. At $z\sim10$, cold streams feed a compact galaxy ($R_{\rm e}\sim1\rm kpc$), with stellar and surface densities ($>10^5\rm cm^{-3}$, $>10^5\rm M_\odot pc^{-2}$) exceeding FFB thresholds. The global star-formation efficiency (SFE) is $\varepsilon_s\sim0.2\text{--}0.3$, associated with a fluctuating star-formation history. We identified over $10^5$ star clusters ($M_{\star}>10^{4.5}\rm M_\odot$) with a nearly scale-free mass distribution (${\rm d}N/{{\rm d}\log M}\propto M^{-1.06}$). Approximately 90\% of star formation occurs in clusters, which at a given time constitute $30\text{--}40\%$ of the total stellar mass. The star formation in most of the clusters of masses $<10^7\rm M_\odot$, occurs in bursts of $<3\rm Myr$ and a local SFE $\sim0.5\pm 0.2$. Cluster metallicities ($-2.01<\log (Z/Z_\odot)<-0.45$) indicate rapid baryon recycling. Feedback-driven outflows exhibit typical temperature of $10^7\rm K$ and typical velocities of $\sim 2000\rm km\ s^{-1}$. In the highly dynamic central $1\rm kpc$, clusters undergo rapid orbital decay and merge to assemble the oblate nuclear stellar cluster. Cluster shapes range from oblate to prolate, with a triaxial median. These clusters are consistent with JWST observations, and a fraction of them may survive to yield the globular clusters (GCs) at low redshifts.

### [12] [Carbon Abundances in Metal-Poor Stars Reveal Distinct Galaxy and Star Formation Pathways in the Early Universe](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12617)
*Alexander Yelland,Anna Frebel,Xiaowei Ou,Sarah Hughes,Mohammad K. Mardini*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文通过汇总1032颗贫金属恒星的碳丰度数据，分析了不同银河系卫星星系中碳增强贫金属（CEMP）恒星的分布规律，揭示了矮星系质量与CEMP分数之间的新关系，并探讨了早期恒星形成机制及银河系晕的并合历史。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: CEMP恒星保存了早期化学增丰、低质量恒星形成和星系等级并合的重要信息，但其在不同星系系统中的分布特征尚不清晰。

Method: 整合来自银河系晕、超微弱矮星系（UFDs）、经典矮椭球星系、吸积矮星系、小吸积恒星系统（SASS）及恒星流等多类系统的1032颗恒星碳丰度数据，统计各系统CEMP星比例，并结合[M_V]与CEMP分数、[C/H]丰度分析其物理起源。

Result: 发现低质量UFDs在低金属丰度下CEMP比例高，而大质量经典矮星系比例低，确立了M_V–CEMP分数关系；部分恒星落在理论‘禁戒区’内，暗示尘埃冷却参与早期恒星形成；银河系贫金属晕由多种矮星系并合而成，CEMP星主要来自早期UFD类系统，非CEMP星则源于中等质量晕系统。

Conclusion: CEMP星的分布反映了不同质量矮星系的恒星形成与反馈历史，支持矮星系质量决定其早期化学演化路径的观点，并为银河系组装历史提供了关键约束。

Abstract: Carbon-enhanced metal-poor (CEMP; with $\rm{[Fe/H]} \le -2.0$ and $\rm{[C/Fe]} \ge 0.7$) stars preserve information about early chemical enrichment, low-mass star formation, and the hierarchical assembly of galaxies. In this study, we have compiled an extensive literature sample of 1032 stellar carbon abundances spanning the metal-poor Milky Way halo (437 stars), 21 ultra-faint dwarf galaxies (UFDs; 102 stars), seven classical dwarf spheroidal galaxies (254 stars), three accreted dwarf galaxies (90 stars), the Small Accreted Stellar Systems (SASS; 77 stars), and eleven stellar streams (72 stars). We establish the fractions of CEMP stars for each of these systems and categories. Generally, the low-mass UFDs possess the high fractions at low metallicities, whereas the more massive classical dwarf galaxies have relatively few CEMP stars. This behavior reveals a new low-metallicity Magnitude ($M_{\rm V}$)--CEMP Fraction relation across the dwarf satellite galaxy population. The high CEMP fractions in surviving UFDs suggest their enrichment was dominated by faint supernovae, as higher energy input would likely have quenched star production. The low CEMP fractions in classical dwarfs imply predominantly in situ formation rather than assembly from smaller systems. Using $\rm{[C/H]}$ abundances, we also probe early low-mass star formation. Eight stars lie within or near the theoretical ''forbidden zone'', indicating that dust-induced cooling, alongside fine-structure line cooling, contributed to early star formation. These rare dust-cooled stars may have formed in UFD-like systems that did not survive. Overall, the metal-poor Milky Way halo appears to have assembled from many different dwarf galaxies, with CEMP halo stars being contributed by early UFD-like systems and non-CEMP halo stars by intermediate-sized halos that later formed classical dwarfs.

### [13] [The X-ray photon index Eddington ratio relation in radio-quiet quasars from XMM-Newton and SDSS](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12668)
*SH. M. Shehata,Baraa Hany,Reham Mostafa*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本研究通过对642个类星体进行X射线光谱分析，发现射电宁静类星体的光子指数Γ与爱丁顿比λ_Edd存在显著正相关，支持盘-冕耦合模型，并揭示了λ_Edd随红移增加、随黑洞质量减小的普适趋势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 建立并刻画射电宁静类星体中光子指数（Γ）与爱丁顿比（λ_Edd）之间的基本关系，探究吸积物理、喷流活动与类星体宇宙学演化的关联。

Method: 交叉匹配XMM-Newton DR11与SDSS DR16类星体样本，经严格质量筛选与自动光谱还原，获取可靠Γ和2–10 keV本征光度；结合多波段数据分类RQ/RL类星体；利用吸收校正X射线数据与动力学黑洞质量估算λ_Edd；统计检验Γ–λ_Edd及相关演化依赖关系。

Result: RQ类星体平均Γ≈2.0、log λ_Edd≈−1.2；Γ与λ_Edd呈显著正相关；λ_Edd随红移z升高而增大，随黑洞质量M_BH增大而减小，与近期独立研究高度一致。

Conclusion: X射线谱斜率与吸积率的关联为盘-冕耦合提供了观测支持，且RQ类星体的吸积特性具有普适的宇宙学演化规律，暗示其物理机制在大尺度上具有一致性。

Abstract: This study presents a comprehensive X-ray spectroscopic analysis of 642 quasars, obtained by cross-matching the XMM-Newton Serendipitous Source Catalog (DR11) with the Sloan Digital Sky Survey (DR16) quasar catalog. After stringent quality filtering and automated spectral reduction, we derived reliable photon indices ($Γ$) and intrinsic 2--10 keV X-ray luminosities. Using multiwavelength data, sources were classified into 561 radio-quiet (RQ) and 81 radio-loud (RL) quasars. We estimate the bolometric luminosity and Eddington ratio ($λ_{\mathrm{Edd}}$) from absorption-corrected X-ray measurements and virial black hole masses. Our primary objective is to establish and characterize the fundamental relationship between the photon index and Eddington ratio for RQ population. We find that RQ quasars exhibit systematically higher Eddington ratios, peaking at $\log λ_{\mathrm{Edd}} \approx -1.2$, and softer spectra with $Γ\approx 2.0$. A statistically significant positive correlation between $Γ$ and $λ_{\mathrm{Edd}}$ is detected in RQ quasars, supporting disk--corona coupling models. To validate our results within the broader context of AGN evolution, we further examine the dependence of $λ_{\mathrm{Edd}}$ on redshift ($z$) and black hole mass ($M_{\mathrm{BH}}$). For RQ quasars, $λ_{\mathrm{Edd}}$ increases with redshift and decreases with $M_{\mathrm{BH}}$, in strong agreement with recent results \cite{aggarwal2024evidence}, highlighting the universal nature of these accretion trends. By correlating spectral slope with accretion rate, this work provides new insights into the interplay between accretion physics, jet activity, and the cosmic evolution of quasars.

### [14] [The $M_{\rm BH}$$-$$R_{\rm b}$ relation and the high-mass end of the $M_{\rm BH}$$-$$σ$ relation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12669)
*Bililign Dullo*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文利用151个具有动力学测量黑洞质量的星系样本，研究了黑洞质量与恒星速度弥散度σ及核心尺寸Rb之间的标度关系；发现大核心星系在MBH-σ关系中呈现高黑洞质量端的显著上翘，且MBH-Rb关系比MBH-σ关系具有更小的弥散度，支持多次干并合驱动超大质量黑洞增长的模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解超大质量黑洞与其宿主星系之间的协同演化关系，特别是高黑洞质量端偏离经典MBH-σ关系的物理起源，以及核心结构参数Rb是否能提供更稳健的黑洞质量示踪。

Method: 基于151个动力学测量黑洞质量的星系样本，分别拟合MBH-σ和MBH-Rb（限于30个core-Sérsic星系）标度关系；区分Sérsic、normal-core与large-core星系子样本，分析其在各关系中的分布与偏离，并结合干并合模型解释高质端上翘现象。

Result: 得到更新的MBH ∝ Rb^(1.16±0.10)关系（rms≈0.28 dex）；Sérsic与normal-core星系共同满足MBH-σ斜率为4.95±0.29的线性关系（rms≈0.46 dex）；large-core星系在高MBH端显著上翘，偏离达1–4倍本征弥散（0.39 dex）；MBH-Rb关系比对应MBH-σ关系弥散低30–47%。

Conclusion: MBH-Rb关系比MBH-σ关系更紧密，表明核心尺寸是比速度弥散更稳健的超大质量黑洞质量示踪；高黑洞质量端的MBH-σ上翘源于多次主要干并合，该过程同时导致σ-LV关系在亮端变平，支持并合驱动黑洞与星系联合演化的图景。

Abstract: Using a sample of 151 galaxies with dynamically measured black hole (BH) masses ($M_{\rm BH}$), we investigate the scaling relations between $M_{\rm BH}$ and the stellar velocity dispersion, $σ$, and, for a subsample of 30 core-Sérsic galaxies, between $M_{\rm BH}$ and the size of the partially depleted core, $R_{\rm b}$. Core-Sérsic galaxies, identified using high-resolution $Hubble ~ Space ~ Telescope$ imaging and spanning both the normal-core $(R_{\rm b}<0.5$ kpc) and large-core ($R_{\rm b}>0.5$ kpc) regimes, define an updated $M_{\rm BH}$$-$$R_{\rm b}$ relation of the form $M_{\rm BH} \propto R_{\rm b}^{1.16 \pm 0.10}$, with an rms scatter of $Δ_{\rm rms} \simeq 0.28$ dex in $\log M_{\rm BH}$. We find that Sérsic and normal-core galaxies together follow a common log-linear $M_{\rm BH}$-$σ$ relation with a slope of $4.95 \pm 0.29$ and a scatter $Δ_{\rm rms} \simeq 0.46$ dex. Deviations from this relation arise at the highest BH masses, where large-core galaxies, including six with direct $M_{\rm BH}$ measurements, drive a significant upturn. We find that these galaxies typically host ultramassive black holes whose masses scale more strongly with $R_{\rm b}$ than $σ$, and lie $\sim (1-4$) $~\times$ the intrinsic scatter (0.39 dex) above the relation defined by Sérsic and normal-core galaxies. The $M_{\rm BH}$$-$$R_{\rm b}$ relation shows $\sim 30$-$47\%$ less scatter in $\log M_{\rm BH}$ than the corresponding $M_{\rm BH}$$-$$σ$ relation for the same sample. We interpret the high-mass upturn in the $M_{\rm BH}$$-$$σ$ diagram as a consequence of successive major, dry mergers, a scenario that naturally explains the observed flattening of the $σ-L_V$ relation at $M_V < -23.5$ mag.

</details>


### [15] [Unprecedented Constraints on Gas Flows at High Redshift Using Deep JWST/NIRSpec Observations from the LyC22, EXCELS, and AURORA Surveys](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12686)
*Emily Kehoe,Alice E. Shapley,Adam C. Carnall,Fergus Cullen,Thomas M. Stanton,Daniel Schaerer,Rui Marques-Chaves,Charles C. Steidel,Ryan L. Sanders,Natalie Lam,Karla Z. Arellano-Cordova,Ryan Begley,Sophia R. Flury,Natalia G. Guseva,Timothy Heckman,Alaina Henry,Akio K. Inoue,Yuri I. Izotov,Ho-Hin Leung,Derek J. McLeod,Kate Rowlands,Alberto Saldana-Lopez,Dirk Scholte,Maya Skarbinski,Struan D. Stevenson,Elizabeth Taylor,Bingjie Wang,Naveen A. Reddy*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本研究利用JWST/NIRSpec观测z~3星系的Fe II、Mg II和Na D吸收线，分析低电离气体外流与星系内禀性质及视线倾角的关系，发现外流速度与星系性质无显著相关性，但探测到外流的星系倾向于更高恒星质量、SFR和面密度；Mg II发射更易在低质量、低消光、高比SFR星系中出现；首次在z~3发现吸收线性质随星系倾角变化：面朝星系吸收更强、外流速度更高，侧向星系更常探测到吸积气体。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究z~3典型恒星形成星系中低电离气体流（外流/吸积）如何依赖于星系内禀属性（如恒星质量、SFR、消光等）和观测视角（倾角），以理解星系反馈与气体循环机制。

Method: 基于JWST/NIRSpec对LyC22、EXCELS和AURORA巡天中总计176（Fe II）、197（Mg II）、315（Na D）个z~3星系的近紫外至光学吸收线观测，结合单个谱与叠加谱分析，统计检验外流速度与星系参数的相关性，并按倾角分组比较吸收强度与运动学特征。

Result: 未发现外流速度与星系质量、SFR等参数的显著统计相关；有外流探测的星系整体偏向更高质量、SFR和Σ_SFR；Mg II发射偏好低质量、低A_V、高sSFR星系；首次在z~3发现吸收线强度与外流速度随倾角系统变化：面朝星系吸收更强、外流更快，侧向星系更常探测到吸积信号。

Conclusion: z~3星系中气体外流方向大致垂直于盘面，而冷气体吸积更倾向沿盘面发生，该几何结构与低红移观测及宇宙学模拟预测一致，支持星系风与冷吸积共存的双模气体循环图像。

Abstract: We investigate how low-ionization gas flows in typical star-forming galaxies at $z\sim3$ depend on galaxy intrinsic properties and viewing angle. For this analysis we use JWST/NIRSpec observations of rest-frame near-UV Fe II and Mg II absorption, and rest-frame optical Na D absorption. This study combines galaxies from the LyC22, EXCELS, and AURORA surveys and contains 176, 197, and 315 galaxies, respectively, with Fe II, Mg II, and Na D coverage. Based on both individual and composite spectra, we find no statistically significant correlations between outflow velocity and galaxy properties. However, galaxies with detected outflows tend towards higher stellar masses, SFR, and $Σ_{\rm SFR}$ than those without outflows, suggesting that the two samples are not drawn from the same parent population. Finally, we additionally find that Mg II emission is preferentially detected in galaxies with lower stellar mass and $A_V$, and higher sSFR, consistent with conditions that favor the escape of resonantly scattered line and ionizing continuum radiation. We present the first evidence in $z\sim3$ star-forming galaxies that properties of the absorption lines depend on galaxy inclination, with more face-on systems showing stronger absorption and higher outflow velocities, while inflowing gas is more frequently detected in more highly inclined galaxies. These trends are consistent with observations at $z\lesssim1$ and predictions from cosmological simulations in which galactic winds are launched perpendicular to the galactic disks, while accretion occurs primarily along the disk plane.

### [16] [Supermassive Black Hole Assembly from Heavy Seeds with Dynamical Friction in the BRAHMA Simulations: Implications for JWST, LISA, and the Local Universe](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12851)
*Aklant K. Bhowmick,Laura Blecha,Paul Torrey,Luke Zoltan Kelley,Rachel S. Somerville,Rainer Weinberger,Priyamvada Natarajan,Tiziana Di Matteo,Lars Hernquist,Mark Vogelsberger,Alex M. Garcia*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文利用BRAHMA宇宙学模拟，研究不同重种子形成模型（宽松vs严格）对高红移（z~5）超大质量黑洞种群的影响，发现宽松模型能更好解释JWST观测到的早期超大质量黑洞，并预测可观测的引力波事件率和本地黑洞占据率以区分种子形成机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: JWST在z≳5处发现超大质量黑洞，亟需理解其种子起源；现有模型对种子形成条件假设差异大，需通过可观测预言加以区分。

Method: 基于[18–72 Mpc]³ BRAHMA宇宙学模拟，引入亚网格动力摩擦模型，对比两类宽松种子模型（所有满足致密、贫金属气体条件的晕均形成~10⁴或~10⁵ M⊙种子）与一类严格种子模型（仅满足直接坍缩黑洞形成额外条件时才形成~10⁵ M⊙种子）。

Result: 宽松模型在z~5产生更多大质量黑洞，可解释JWST观测到的高光度（~10⁴³–10⁴⁵ erg s⁻¹）系统，并预测高引力波并合率（≳100 yr⁻¹）和近100%本地黑洞占据率（即使在M_* ≲ 10⁷ M⊙星系中）；严格模型则给出低并合率（~1 yr⁻¹）和低占据率（≲10%，M_* ≲ 10⁸ M⊙）。

Conclusion: JWST观测到的高红移超大质量黑洞更支持宽松的重种子形成模型；未来引力波探测和本地黑洞占据率测量将成为判别黑洞种子起源的关键观测依据。

Abstract: The JWST discoveries of supermassive black holes (BHs) at $z \gtrsim 5$ may provide key insights into their seeding origins. Using new $[18{-}72~\rm Mpc]^3$ BRAHMA cosmological simulations, we investigate how variations in heavy-seed prescriptions, coupled with a subgrid dynamical friction model, shape BH populations at $z \sim 5$ and $z \sim 0$. We consider two "lenient'' seed models, in which all halos containing sufficient dense & metal-poor gas form $\sim10^4$ and $\sim10^5~M_{\odot}$ seeds, and a "strict'' seed model, in which $\sim10^5 M_{\odot}$ seeds form only under additional constraints motivated by direct collapse black hole formation. By $z \sim 5$, all models produce $M_*-M_{\rm BH}$ relations broadly consistent with the observed local Universe for $M_*\gtrsim10^9~M_{\odot}$ galaxies, but only the lenient scenarios generate systems near the upper envelope of the observed local scatter. In galaxies hosting $M_{\rm BH} \sim 10^8$-$10^9~M_{\odot}$ BHs, lenient production of $\sim10^5~M_{\odot}$ seeds also produces multiple overmassive systems with $M_{\rm BH}/M_* \gtrsim 0.01$. Although their growth is dominated by seeding and mergers, these systems reach luminosities of $\sim10^{43}$-$10^{45}\mathrm{erg s^{-1}}$, comparable to those inferred for JWST-detected BHs. As a key observational signature, the lenient seed models yield merger rates of $\gtrsim100\mathrm{yr^{-1}}$ and near-unity local BH occupation fractions even in galaxies with $M_* \lesssim 10^7~M_{\odot}$. In contrast, the strict seed model produces merger rates of only $\sim1\mathrm{yr^{-1}}$ and local occupation fractions of $\lesssim10\%$ for galaxies with $M_* \lesssim 10^8~M_{\odot}$. Future gravitational-wave event rates and measurements of local BH occupation fractions will therefore provide strong constraints on the dominant pathways responsible for high-redshift BH assembly.

### [17] [SIDM and CDM interpretations of the million-solar-mass lensing perturber JVAS B1938+666-$\mathcal{V}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12909)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用引力热流体模拟，研究自相互作用暗物质（SIDM）晕在深度核心坍缩阶段的演化行为，并对比冷暗物质（CDM）模型引入中间质量黑洞及潮汐剥离机制的可能性。

Conclusion: JVAS B1938+666中致密天体的结构更支持自相互作用暗物质（SIDM）模型，对冷暗物质（CDM）构成挑战，尤其质疑其在小尺度上能否自然产生此类高密度结构。

Abstract: A $10^6\,M_\odot$ object has recently been inferred from gravitational imaging of the strong-lensing system JVAS B1938+666, exhibiting an unusually dense inner region embedded within an extended envelope, far exceeding expectations for cold dark matter (CDM) halos. Using gravothermal fluid simulations, we show that such a structure arises naturally in self-interacting dark matter (SIDM) halos evolving into a deep core-collapse phase, where a secondary dense central core forms within an extended profile. The resulting density structure closely matches the inferred properties of the lensing object. We also demonstrate that a similar profile could be reproduced in CDM in the presence of an intermediate-mass black hole, but this requires an early-forming progenitor that subsequently loses $5$ orders of magnitude in mass through tidal stripping by the lens galaxy. Whether such a scenario can be realized in realistic cosmological environments remains an open question.

### [18] [Chemical signatures from the first stars embedded in metal-poor gas in galaxies at cosmic dawn](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13078)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 分析JWST-SPURS巡天获取的三个z≈7.8–9.3星系的近红外中分辨率吸收光谱，测量金属吸收线丰度比（如[C/O]），并与发射线结果对比；同时检验更大样本星系平均谱中的共性特征。

Result: 发现吸收线显示气体金属丰度远低于发射线所测值，且所有目标均呈现超太阳[C/O]比；该特征在更高统计量的相似红移星系平均谱中亦存在。

Abstract: The first generation of stars formed from pristine, neutral hydrogen gas. The most massive of these exploded as supernovae within a few million years of their birth, producing the first heavier elements and leaving distinct chemical signatures of their origin in the surrounding medium. However, chemical abundance studies have so far mainly relied on emission-line measurements, which are luminosity weighted and hence biased towards the most recently formed stars. Here we analyse near-infrared, medium-resolution spectroscopy from the JWST-SPURS program of three UV-bright galaxies at redshifts 7.8, 8.6, and 9.3, within the first 650 to 520 million years after the Big Bang. The chemical abundance patterns of the metal lines detected in absorption hint at extremely metal-poor gas, substantially lower than inferred from the emission lines tracing the central, star-forming regions. Further, they all exhibit super-solar [C/O] abundances, which is also imprinted in the averaged spectrum of a larger set of galaxies at similar redshifts. These results reveal the distinct chemical signatures of the first Population III supernovae explosions.

### [19] [Grain Alignment and Dust Evolution Physics with Polarisation (GRADE-POL). II. On the physical basis of Serkowski and super-Serkowski polarisation spectra](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13123)
*Le Ngoc Tram,Thiem Hoang,B-G Andersson,Alex Lazarian,Lapo Fanciullo,Bao Truong,Archana Soam*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文重新审视了星际偏振的Serkowski关系及其在紫外波段的异常（super-Serkowski），通过结合顺磁弛豫（DG）与辐射扭矩（RAT）对尘埃颗粒的定向机制，成功拟合了四颗恒星的观测数据；发现B型星辐射（尤其Lyman极限以下）增强RAT可解释super-Serkowski现象，而典型星际辐射场下仅RAT即可解释标准Serkowski谱，为未来紫外波段偏振观测提供理论支持。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 约25%的星际偏振谱在中紫外波段呈现超出经典Serkowski关系的偏振度增强（super-Serkowski），传统模型难以统一解释，亟需结合更完善的尘埃取向物理机制。

Method: 基于顺磁弛豫（DG）和辐射扭矩（RAT）协同作用的尘埃取向模型，利用HD 30614、HD 204827、HD 37903和HD 161056的观测数据进行约束，并分别采用缩放后的星际辐射场和B型星辐射场两种辐射环境开展拟合分析。

Result: B型星辐射（λ<912 Å）增强RAT可合理解释HD 30614和HD 204827的super-Serkowski谱，联合DG机制进一步改善λ⁻¹≥5.5 μm⁻¹处拟合；而HD 37903和HD 161056的标准Serkowski谱仅需典型星际辐射场下的RAT机制即可解释，DG机制贡献极弱。

Conclusion: RAT与DG机制的联合模型能统一解释从红外到远紫外的恒星光偏振谱，特别是揭示了B型星紫外辐射在驱动超Serkowski偏振中的关键作用，为未来紫外偏振巡天任务提供可靠理论框架。

Abstract: Optical-to-near infrared interstellar polarisation, induced by aligned dust grains, generally follows a convex wavelength dependence, known as the Serkowski relation. However, observations in the ultraviolet (UV) and at [mid-]infrared wavelengths indicated that some of the spectra do not follow this relation. Specifically, about 25% show an excess in the degree of polarisation at mid-UV wavelengths ($λ^{-1} > 3\,\rm μm^{-1}$), referred to as the super-Serkowski polarisation. In this study, we re-examine both the Serkowski and super-Serkowski spectra based on the joint effect of paramagnetic relaxation (DG alignment) and radiative torque (RAT) alignment. We used the observational data for HD 30614, HD 204827, HD 37903 and HD 161056 to constrain our modelling. We examined two types of radiation fields: one derived from the scaled interstellar radiation field and another originating from a B-type star. For the super-Serkowski spectra of HD 30614 and HD 204827, our model demonstrates that RAT alignment enhanced by radiation produced from a B-type star below the Lyman limit ($λ=912 Å$) can reasonably explain the observations and that a combination with the DG alignments results in a better fit for $λ^{-1}\geq 5.5\,\rm μm^{-1}$. For the Serkowski spectra in HD 37903 and HD 161056, only RAT alignment by itself under the typical interstellar radiation field above the Lyman limit, within a typical cold neutral medium, can account for the observed spectra, with a combination of a very inefficient DG alignment. The capacity of our model to predict the starlight polarisation spectrum up to from infrared to far-UV is thus a promising tool for interpreting future missions that observe spectrophotometry in the UV bands.

### [20] [Direct detection of cool molecular gas in a star-forming galaxy at $z=7.31$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13393)
*Karin Cescon,Jacqueline A. Hodge,Leindert A. Boogaard,Hiddo S. B. Algera,Lucie E. Rowland,Dominik A. Riechers,Renske Smit,Ilse De Looze,Rychard Bouwens,Paul van der Werf,Manuel Aravena,Elisabete da Cunha,Pratika Dayal,Andrea Ferrara,Rebecca Fisher,Hanae Inami,Pavel E. Mancera Piña,Pascal A. Oesch,Andrea Pallottini,Matus Rybak,Sander Schouws,Laura Sommovigo,Mauro Stefanon,Livia Vallini*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文研究了红移z=7.31的星系REBELS-25的分子气体含量和星际介质（ISM）条件，首次在z>7探测到低-J CO谱线（CO(3-2)），确认其拥有极高质量的气体储备，并通过多谱线建模独立推断分子气体质量，同时提出[C II]在再电离时期仍可作为可靠的分子气体示踪剂。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索宇宙早期（再电离时期）大质量星系中分子气体的含量与物理条件，检验低-J CO谱线在高红移下的可探测性及常用气体示踪剂（如CO、[C I]、[C II]）的适用性。

Method: 利用VLA Q波段与ALMA Band 3深度观测获取CO(3-2)、CO(7-6)及[C I](2-1)数据；结合CMB修正的CO流量估算分子气体质量；采用辐射转移代码TUNER对CO与尘埃连续谱进行自洽建模，规避r31和α_CO假设；联合CO与[C II]观测推导经验性α_[C II]转换因子。

Result: 首次在z=7.31（宇宙年龄约7亿年）探测到CO(3-2)，测得分子气体质量M_mol ≈ (1.0±0.4)×10¹¹ M⊙（依赖α_CO假设）或(1.8⁺¹·⁰₋₀·₉)×10¹¹ M⊙（模型独立）；气体分数f_gas≈0.95，气体尘埃比δ_GDR≈6×10²，耗尽时标τ_dep≈1.2 Gyr；推得α_[C II] = (60±25) M⊙/L⊙。

Conclusion: 低-J CO谱线在z>7仍可观测，证实早期星系具备巨量冷气体储备；[C II]在再电离时期仍是有效的H₂示踪剂；结果支持主序星系标度关系向高红移外推，并为下一代望远镜开展高红移分子气体普查奠定基础。

Abstract: We investigate the molecular gas content and interstellar medium (ISM) conditions of REBELS-25, a massive, star-forming galaxy at $z=7.31$. Deep VLA Q-band and ALMA Band 3 observations reveal CO(3-2) and CO(7-6) emission (both at $\sim3.5σ$), and provide an upper limit on [C I](2-1). From the CMB-corrected CO(3-2) flux-representing the highest-redshift detection of a low-$J$ CO transition to date-we derive a molecular gas mass of $M_{\rm mol}=(1.0\pm0.4)\times10^{11}\,(α_{\rm CO}/(3\,$M$_{\odot}$(K$\,$\kms$\,$pc$^2)^{-1}))\,$M$_{\odot}$, directly confirming the presence of a very massive gas reservoir only $\simeq700\,$Myr after the Big Bang. This implies an extreme gas fraction of $f_{\rm gas}\simeq0.95$, a gas-to-dust ratio of $δ_{\rm GDR}\simeq6\times10^2$, and a depletion timescale of $τ_{\rm dep}\simeq1.2\,$Gyr, broadly consistent with extrapolated scaling relations for main-sequence galaxies at lower redshift. Using the radiative transfer code TUNER, we self-consistently model CO and dust continuum emission in the context of the significant CMB background, constraining ISM properties and recovering $M_{\rm mol}= (1.8^{+1.0}_{-0.9})\times10^{11}\,$M$_{\odot}$, independent of assumptions about $r_{31}$ and $α_{\rm CO}$. We further discuss the use of alternative molecular gas tracers at early epochs. Combining CO and [C II] measurements, we infer an empirical [C II]-to-H$_2$ conversion factor of $α_{\rm [C II]}=(60\pm25)\,$M$_{\odot}$/L$_{\odot}$, suggesting [C II] remains a viable molecular gas tracer in the Epoch of Reionization. These results demonstrate the detectability of low-$J$ CO emission even at $z>7$, paving the way for next-generation facilities, and provide critical insights into the rapid mass assembly of galaxies during the first billion years of cosmic history.

### [21] [Beyond the Fundamental Metallicity Relation: galaxy sizes encode the link between inflow and metallicity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13124)
*N. F. Boardman,V. Wild,D. Scholte,K. Wang,N. Vale Asari,A. Saintonge*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文通过结合MaNGA光谱、HI-MaNGA气体质量和DynPop动力学质量数据，发现内区气体质量是除恒星质量外预测气体金属丰度的最重要参数；揭示了星系尺寸与金属丰度残差的关系源于长期吸积历史差异，而非短期气体流入扰动。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 以往研究分别发现质量-金属丰度关系（MZR）残差与恒星形成率、气体质量及光学尺寸存在反相关，但缺乏对三者联合影响的系统分析。

Method: 利用MaNGA积分场光谱、HI-MaNGA气体质量和DynPop动力学质量，对约1500个恒星形成星系进行联合统计分析，并结合化学演化模型解释观测趋势。

Result: 内区气体质量是继恒星质量后预测气体金属丰度的最关键参数；星系尺寸与内区气体质量强相关；紧凑星系具有更低的动力学质量与更早的吸积历史，导致晚期气体储库更快衰减和更高金属丰度。

Conclusion: 在固定恒星质量下，星系尺寸编码了晕组装历史、长期气体吸积历史、当前气体储量与金属丰度之间的内在联系，支持金属丰度由长期吸积历史主导而非瞬时过程。

Abstract: Gas-phase chemical abundances are key observable consequences of galaxy evolution, being intrinsically tied to galaxy formation histories. Gas metallicity rises with increasing stellar mass ($\mathrm{M_*}$), forming the well-known mass-metallicity relation (MZR). MZR residuals have separately been shown to anti-correlate with star-formation rate (the ``fundamental'' metallicity relation), with gas mass and with optical size, but no single analysis has considered all trends together. We thus perform a combined analysis of all three trends, utilizing optical MaNGA integral field spectroscopy, HI-MaNGA gas masses, and MaNGA DynPop dynamical masses. We estimate inner gas masses for $\sim$1500 star-forming galaxies, finding this to be the most important parameter after $\mathrm{M_*}$ in predicting gas metallicities. We obtain equivalent results for stellar metallicities and gaseous N/O, suggesting that current inner gas masses are intrinsically linked to long-term chemical evolution histories. We show that more compact galaxies have lower dynamical masses, challenging suggestions that deeper gravitational potentials confer higher metallicities. We find a strong correlation between inner gas mass and galaxy size, meaning that short term inflow fluctuations cannot be responsible for the MZR residuals. With chemical evolution models, we show that our results can instead be explained by differences in long-term inflow histories. The earlier inflow histories of compact galaxies lead to lower gas masses and more rapidly declining gas reservoirs at late times, leading to higher metallicities. At fixed stellar mass, galaxy size therefore encodes the link between halo assembly histories, long-term gas inflow histories, current gas reservoirs and metallicity.

</details>


### [22] [Basis sets and Coulomb resolutions in rotational coordinates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13324)
*Edward Lilley*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文利用广义拉普拉斯对称算子，在多种可分离坐标系（包括两种R-可分离系统）中构建基组或库仑分解，拓展了基组构造适用的几何范围，并给出了若干闭式解析表达。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 拓展基组构造在不同几何构型中的适用性，以服务于星系动力学和计算化学等领域的需求。

Method: 基于广义拉普拉斯对称算子，在可分离（含R-可分离）坐标系中构造基组；推导出多个具闭式解（单个Jacobi多项式表达）的基组；建立球极/长球坐标基组到双球坐标/环面坐标基组的变换方法。

Result: 得到三个闭式基组（两个在长球坐标、一个在柱坐标），并实现了球极/长球坐标基组向双球/环面坐标基组的系统性转换。

Conclusion: 广义拉普拉斯对称算子为多类坐标系下基组构造提供了统一框架，显著扩展了几何适用范围，且具备实际计算价值。

Abstract: Using generalised Laplacian symmetry operators, we construct basis sets or Coulomb resolutions in several separable coordinate systems, including two R-separable systems. This expands the possible geometries in which basis set construction is feasible, a problem which is relevant to both galactic dynamics and computational chemistry. In particular we derive three basis sets (two in prolate spheroidal and one in cylindrical coordinates) which are expressible in closed-form using a single Jacobi polynomial. We also show how any spherical polar or prolate spheroidal basis set may be transformed into a bispherical or toroidal basis set.

</details>


### [23] [Galaxy clusters in the VIDEO fields: detection and characterisation in the context of MOONRISE](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13359)
*Pierre Galois,Christophe Benoist,Gianluca Castignani,Matteo Maturi,Sophie Maurogordato,Pascale Jablonka,Yannick Bahé,Derek McLeod,Rebecca Bowler,Olga Cucciati,Lauro Moscardini,Manuela Magliocchetti,Mario Radovich,Michele Cirasuolo,Giovani Covone,Fergus Cullen,Callum Donnan,Hector Flores,William Hartley,Roberto Maiolino,Ross McLure,Nicolarosario Napolitano,Maurizio Paolillo,Mattia Vaccari*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文利用AMICO和WaZP光度红移星系团探测器，在XMM-LSS和CDFS VIDEO区域识别出519个z=0.1–3的星系团候选体（含74个z>1.5），并结合光谱红移、BCG识别、成员概率与颜色-星等图红序分析，验证其高红移演化模型，并评估MOONRISE巡天策略对这些星系团的探测能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为支持即将开展的MOONRISE巡天，需提前评估其对高红移星系团的探测能力，并理解z>1.5星系团中红序星系的形成与演化。

Method: 使用AMICO和WaZP两种光度红移星系团探测算法，在XMM-LSS和CDFS VIDEO约4.5 deg²区域内联合探测星系团；识别BCG、计算成员概率；交叉匹配光谱红移数据（共320个有z_spec）；分析红序特征并与被动演化模型对比；模拟不同MOONRISE观测策略下的探测与证认效率。

Result: 获得519个一致探测的星系团候选体（74个z>1.5）；光度红移与光谱红移吻合良好；红序成分支持高红移（z~2–3）形成+被动演化的模型；MOONRISE最浅策略下仍可高效完成z∼1.7以内星系团的光谱证认与表征。

Conclusion: 该工作不仅构建了迄今较完备的z>1.5星系团候选样本，还证实MOONRISE具备在z∼1.7开展高红移星系团物理性质研究的能力，为理解致密环境中星系形成提供了关键观测基础。

Abstract: We analyse the cluster content of the $\sim 4.5 \text{ deg}^{2}$ XMM-LSS and CDFS VIDEO fields which are expected to be partially covered by the upcoming MOONRISE survey. Using AMICO and WaZP photometric redshift-based cluster finders, we construct a sample of $519$ cluster candidates detected by both finders in the redshift range $z = 0.1-3$, including $74$ detections at $z > 1.5$. For all detections, we identify the Brightest Central Galaxy (BCG) and compute a list of probabilistic cluster memberships. Our photometric redshift measurements of the clusters agree well with spectroscopic redshifts from the literature, when available. From ancillary spectroscopic data, we assign $z_\text{spec}$ measurements to $116$ cluster candidates based on their spectroscopic members and to $204$ based on their likely BCGs. We also show that candidates containing Radio-Loud members are efficiently recovered using the prior-based cluster finder PPM. We perform a preliminary analysis of the galaxy content of these candidates, focusing on the Red-Sequence components of their apparent Colour-Magnitude Diagram. By comparing with models of galaxy evolution, we show that this population is consistent with a model of passive evolution with a formation at high redshift, and is already in place at $z = 1.5-2.0$. Finally, our cluster sample is used to evaluate how these clusters would be detected and characterised, according to various MOONRISE strategies. We show that cluster spectroscopic confirmation and characterisation could be efficiently achieved up to $z\sim1.7$ even with the shallowest survey strategy. This open unprecedented insight into the physical properties of high-redshift galaxy clusters and into galaxy formation in dense environments.

### [24] [Feedback in Extragalactic Star Clusters (FEAST): Spectral Energy Distributions and the Physical Properties of Star Clusters in NGC 628 with CIGALE](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13391)
*Sean T. Linden,Angela Adamo,Alex Pedrini,Daniela Calzetti,Helena Faustino Vieira,Bruce E. Elmegreen,John S. Gallagher,Kelsey Johnson,Matteo Messa,Kathryn Grasha,Ana Duarte-Cabral,Arjan Bik,Giacomo Bortolini,Matteo Correnti,Drew Lapeer,Thomas S. -Y. Lai,Goran Ostlin,Linda J. Smith,Monica Tosi*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文利用哈勃和韦布太空望远镜对NGC 628星系的多波段观测，结合CIGALE模型拟合12000多个星团的能谱分布，揭示了年轻星团在尘埃嵌入阶段的演化序列、清除时标及空间分布特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解年轻星团如何从尘埃气体包裹中浮现，及其与周围介质相互作用的反馈机制。

Method: 利用HST与JWST在0.3–7.7 μm波段观测数据，对NGC 628中超过12,000个光学选源及MIRI选源进行SED拟合（使用CIGALE），推导其年龄、质量、消光和尘埃性质。

Result: 发现eYSC-I与eYSC-II分别对应~3–5 Myr演化阶段；PDR清除时标约4 Myr；旋臂内星团更重、更红化；F770W亮源主要对应最年轻、最尘埃遮蔽区域。

Conclusion: JWST联合CIGALE可有效识别并表征短暂嵌入相的新兴年轻星团，为星团形成与反馈过程提供关键约束。

Abstract: With Hubble Space Telescope (HST) and James Webb Space Telescope (JWST) observations of NGC~628 spanning 0.3--7.7\,$μ$m, we fit the spectral energy distributions (SEDs) of over 12,000 optically-selected star clusters, emerging young star clusters (eYSCs), and MIRI-selected sources with \textsc{cigale} to derive their ages, masses, extinctions, and dust properties. We find that near-infrared selected eYSC-I (compact Pa$α$ and 3.3,$μ$m PAH emission) and eYSC-II (compact Pa$α$ and diffuse 3.3,$μ$m PAH emssion) sources peak at $\sim$3--5~Myr, where $\sim 12\%$ of the clusters have an $E(B{-}V)>2$, demonstrating the presence of dust-embedded populations as clusters emerge. Further, the distributions of the fractional polycyclic aromatic hydrocarbon (PAH) abundance ($q_{\mathrm PAH}$) and stellar-to-nebular attenuation ratio ($E(B{-}V)_{\rm \star}/E(B{-}V)_{\rm neb}$) suggest an evolutionary sequence in which sources evolve from eYSC-I to eYSC-II as clusters clear their surrounding dust and gas. The photo-dissociation region (PDR) clearing timescale inferred from the ratio of eYSC-I to optically visible stellar clusters is $\sim$4~Myr. Additionally, we find that star clusters in the spiral arms of NGC 628 are preferentially more massive and more dust-reddened than those in inter-arm regions.~Finally, we find that $\sim$65\% of eYSC-I, $\sim$27\% of eYSC-II, and $\sim$40\% of F335M-selected sources coincide with an F770W peak in our MIRI-selected catalog within 4 pixels, confirming that F770W-bright sources preferentially trace the youngest and dustiest regions. Overall, our results highlight the ability of JWST together with \textsc{cigale} model grids to identify and characterize eYSCs during their short-lived embedded phases, and provide constraints on the feedback mechanisms that govern the emergence of stellar clusters.

</details>


### [25] [The ultra low-frequency spectral properties of bright extended radio galaxies in the 3CRR catalogue](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13493)
*J. M. Boxelaar,F. De Gasperin,M. J. Hardcastle,E. De Rubeis,R. J. van Weeren*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 历史上的超低频（<100 MHz）高分辨率观测匮乏，限制了对射电星系中最古老宇宙线电子种群及其加速物理过程的理解。

Method: 结合LOFAR LBA（58 MHz）、HBA（144 MHz）及RACS（887/943.5/1367.5 MHz）数据，选取22个大角径（≥2.5′）3CRR源，构建谱指数图并利用射电色-色图拟合谱老化模型以约束注入谱指数等参数。

Result: 获得样本的超低频谱指数图；FR I星系核区谱指数约0.5（符合一级费米加速），向瓣区增至>1.0；FR II热点谱指数为0.5–0.9，暗示复杂加速或吸收效应。

Conclusion: 超低频观测显著提升了对射电瓣中电子年龄分布与加速机制的理解，证实FR I与FR II在粒子加速和能量演化上存在系统性差异。

Abstract: Context. Active galactic nuclei (AGN) jets are fundamental drivers of galaxy evolution, injecting kinetic energy into their environments. The large-scale morphology and spectral properties of these radio galaxies are consequences of complex particle acceleration, energy loss, and absorption processes. While the shape of the synchrotron spectrum encodes the plasma's energetic history, understanding the physics of particle acceleration and duty cycles has historically been limited by a lack of well-resolved observations at ultra-low frequencies (< 100 MHz), where the oldest cosmic ray electron populations are traced. Aims. This study aims to perform the first comprehensive multi-frequency analysis of bright extended radio galaxies down to 58 MHz. The goal is to study electron acceleration mechanisms, accurately measure the low-frequency spectral shape, and constrain the injection index for a sample of Fanaroff-Riley (FR) I and II galaxies using spectral ageing models. Methods. Utilising new 58 MHz observations from the LOFAR Low Band Antenna (LBA) combined with LOFAR High Band Antenna (HBA; 144 MHz) and Rapid ASKAP Continuum Survey (RACS, 887 MHz & 943.5 MHz & 1367.5 MHz) data, a sub-sample of 22 extended sources from the 3CRR catalogue was selected, requiring the largest angular size to be at least 2.5'. The analysis involves constructing detailed spectral index maps and utilising radio colour-colour diagrams to interpret spectral shapes and constrain ageing model parameters across the radio lobes. Results. This study presents the ultra-low frequency spectral index maps for this sample. For FR I galaxies, spectral indices range from ~0.5 near the core (consistent with first-order Fermi acceleration) to > 1.0 in the lobes. For FR II galaxies, hotspots exhibit steep low-frequency spectra (0.5 - 0.9), suggesting complex acceleration or absorption effects.

</details>


### [26] [Centrally concentrated star formation in young clusters II: Jet feedback](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13666)
*Adilkhan Assilkhan,Sabrina M. Appel,Bekdaulet Shukirgaliyev,Ernazar Abdikamalov,Simon Portegies Zwart,Eric P. Andersson,Mukhagali Kalambay,Mordecai-Mark Mac Low*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文通过Torch星团形成框架模拟研究原恒星喷流对中心密集分子云中恒星形成效率、时变性、星团结构及早期动力学状态的影响，发现喷流反馈可降低恒星形成效率、引发爆发式恒星形成、产生更延展且亚结构丰富的星团，并使恒星系统束缚更弱；在中心密集初始条件下，含喷流模型更符合观测到的年轻星团Q_2D参数范围。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 原恒星喷流作为最早的恒星反馈形式，其对中心密集分子云中恒星形成和星团组装的影响尚不清楚。

Method: 采用Torch星团形成框架，对质量为2.5×10³太阳质量的中心密集初始云模型进行六组含/不含喷流的对比模拟，并补充一组更高分辨率模拟，结合全局恒星形成诊断与恒星群体的结构及动力学分析。

Result: 含喷流模型恒星形成效率为12–16%，显著低于无喷流模型的19–33%；喷流导致恒星形成呈离散爆发而非连续，形成更延展、具亚结构的星团，且剩余恒星系统束缚更弱、维里参数更高；含喷流模型更符合观测中年轻星团的Q_2D参数分布。

Conclusion: 即使在中心密集分子云中，原恒星喷流仍是关键的早期反馈机制，能有效调控恒星形成效率并塑造新生星团的结构。

Abstract: Protostellar jets are one of the earliest forms of stellar feedback, but their impact on star formation and cluster assembly in centrally concentrated molecular clouds remains poorly understood. We study how protostellar jets affect the star formation efficiency, the temporal variability of star formation, star cluster structure, and the early dynamical state of centrally concentrated, newly forming star clusters using the Torch star cluster formation framework. We adopt a centrally concentrated initial cloud model with mass M = 2.5 x 10^3 solar masses and compare six pairs of simulations with and without protostellar jets, supplemented by one additional higher resolution pair of simulations. We analyze our simulations using global star formation diagnostics together with structural and dynamical measures of the stellar population. Models with jet feedback achieve star formation efficiencies of 12-16%, while the corresponding models without jets yield higher efficiencies of 19-33%. Jets also cause star formation to occur in discrete bursts rather than continuously, to produce more extended and substructured stellar systems, and to leave behind stellar populations that are less tightly bound and have higher virial parameters. In our centrally concentrated initial conditions, runs with jets form stellar systems that better reproduce the observed range of the projected structural parameter Q_2D in young clusters than runs without jets, indicating that protostellar jets are an important early feedback channel even in centrally concentrated clouds that regulates star formation efficiencies and shapes the emerging cluster structure.

### [27] [Observing Cosmic Reheating with the expanded Simons Observatory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12519)

Method: 基于Simons Observatory扩展至六台小口径望远镜后的灵敏度预测，结合r=0.0036和r=0.01两个基准张标比场景，分析其对暴胀模型参数（特别是再加热温度和暴胀子耦合）的限制能力，重点考察平板型暴胀与QCD驱动温暴胀模型。

Result: 在r=0.0036或0.01被观测到的前提下，可确定暴胀能标并估计再加热温度量级；对于QCD温暴胀模型，再加热温度和暴胀子-胶子耦合有望以数个百分点精度被测量。

Conclusion: Simons Observatory升级后具备在实验室尺度上检验暴胀微观机制（如通过轴子实验验证暴胀子性质）的潜力，为连接宇宙学观测与粒子物理实验提供新路径。

Abstract: The Simons Observatory will be extended by three Small Aperture Telescopes by 2027, increasing the total number of these instruments to six. We study the prospects for probing the reheating temperature and the inflaton coupling with this configuration, assuming a discovery of primordial gravitational waves in benchmark scenarios with a tensor-to-scalar ratio r=0.0036 or r=0.01. In popular plateau models of inflation, such an observation would fix the scale of inflation and enable determination of the order of magnitude of the reheating temperature and the inflaton interactions. For QCD-driven Warm Inflation the reheating temperature and inflaton coupling to gluons could, under optimistic assumptions, be measured with a precision of a few percent. Such a measurement would imply a clear prediction for complementary inflaton searches in axion experiments, paving the way toward probing the mechanism responsible for the initial conditions of the hot Big Bang in the laboratory.

### [28] [Dark Matter with a Drag at Low Redshift](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12521)
*Martin Schmaltz,Eashwar N. Sivarajan*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的暗物质模型iDCDM，通过晚期暗物质衰变产生暗辐射并与之发生拖曳作用，从而在低红移（z≲1）下抑制结构增长，以解释fσ₈和弱引力透镜观测与ΛCDM预测的偏差。该模型仅增加两个参数，保持背景演化及CMB、BBN不变，并给出可被DESI、Euclid和Rubin望远镜检验的阶梯状增长抑制特征。当前数据对其有轻微偏好（Δχ² = −2.7 至 −7.6）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期fσ₈和弱透镜观测显示z≲1时线性结构增长率低于ΛCDM预测，亟需能晚期内缓慢增长的暗物质模型。

Method: 构建晚期增强型暗物质-暗辐射拖曳模型；提出具体实现iDCDM：冷暗物质晚期衰变为暗辐射，产生随时间增强的拖曳力；引入两个新参数，保持标准宇宙学约束（BBN、CMB、背景演化）不变。

Result: iDCDM预测f(k,z)呈阶梯状抑制；与当前fσ₈等数据拟合优于ΛCDM（Δχ² = −2.7 至 −7.6），偏好程度依赖于拖曳红移标度及中微子质量假设。

Conclusion: iDCDM为解决低红移结构增长偏低问题提供了简洁、可检验的新机制；其关键预言——k和z分辨的增长率抑制——将由DESI、Euclid和Rubin等下一代巡天决定性检验。

Abstract: Recent analyses of $fσ_8$ and weak-lensing data indicate that the linear growth rate at $z\lesssim 1$ may be lower than predicted by $Λ$CDM. This motivates models of dark matter in which large scale structure growth slows relative to $Λ$CDM at late times. We construct particle models in which dark matter experiences a drag with dark radiation that grows at late times, unlike conventional DM--DR interactions, which fade as the universe expands. A key ingredient is that the radiation interacting with the dark matter is produced at late times from dark matter decay. An explicit model, interacting Decaying Cold Dark Matter (iDCDM), adds two parameters beyond $Λ$CDM while leaving the background, BBN, and primary CMB intact. But it predicts a step-shaped suppression of the linear growth rate $f(k,z)$, a distinctive target for DESI, Euclid, and Rubin. Confronted with current data, iDCDM shows a modest preference over $Λ$CDM, driven by $fσ_8$, with $Δχ^2$ between $-2.7$ and $-7.6$ depending on the assumed scaling of the drag with redshift and on neutrino masses. The decisive test will come from upcoming $k$- and $z$-resolved growth measurements.

</details>


### [29] [Magnetic fields at the dawn of structure formation I. The CARLA J1510+5958 proto-cluster](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12522)
*A. Pagliotta,A. Bonafede,C. Stuardi,C. J. Riseley,D. Vallés-Péerez,P. Tozzi,L. Di Mascolo*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本研究利用JVLA观测z=1.72的CARLA J1510+5958原星系团，通过RM合成与QU拟合分析中心射电噪AGN的法拉第旋转，结合三维模拟，发现原星系际介质（proto-ICM）已被磁化，磁场下限为0.4 μG，证实高红移时期星系团组装早期即存在磁场放大。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解高红移宇宙中磁场的起源、放大机制及强度，特别是原星系团这一星系团形成早期阶段的磁化过程。

Method: 对z=1.72的CARLA J1510+5958原星系团进行JVLA L波段观测，采用RM合成与QU拟合分析AGN偏振辐射的法拉第旋转，并结合不同AGN取向与路径长度的3D湍流磁场与气体密度模拟进行物理解释。

Result: 西部瓣呈现均匀RM（平均−115±32 rad m⁻²），表明局部有序压缩磁场；东部瓣退偏振；RM分布排除纯各向同性随机磁场；QU拟合揭示内部法拉第成分，支持AGN喷流等离子体与周围介质混合并磁化环境；推得proto-ICM磁场下限为0.4 μG。

Conclusion: 在z=1.72已存在被磁化的原星系际介质，证明星系团组装早期即发生磁场放大，AGN在早期磁化过程中起关键作用。

Abstract: Magnetic fields are a fundamental ingredient of the Universe, influencing the formation and evolution of cosmic structures. While magnetic fields in local galaxy clusters have been studied, their origin, amplification, and strength at high redshift are poorly understood. Proto-clusters represent the early stages of galaxy cluster formation, ideal for investigating the early magnetisation of the intra-cluster medium (ICM). We present a study of CARLA J1510+5958 proto-cluster at z = 1.72, observed with the JVLA in the L-band (1-2 GHz). We aim to investigate the magnetic field strength and structure in the proto-ICM and the role of AGN in magnetising the environment during early cluster formation. We analyse Faraday rotation on the polarised emission from the central radio-loud AGN using the Rotation Measure (RM) synthesis and QU fitting technique. We further interpret the observations with 3D simulations of gas density and turbulent magnetic fields, varying AGN orientation and path length. The two AGN lobes show different polarisation properties. The Western lobe exhibits a uniform RM (average $-115 \pm 32\text{ rad m}^{-2}$, dispersion $36 \pm 11\text{ rad m}^{-2}$), indicating a locally ordered magnetic field likely compressed by the lobe, while the Eastern lobe is depolarised. Although the asymmetry indicates a turbulent, magnetised medium, simulations rule out a purely isotropic random field for the Western lobe RM distribution. The QU fitting further suggests an internal Faraday component, interpreted as magnetised relativistic plasma from the lobe mixed with the surrounding gas, indicating possible magnetisation of the ambient medium by the AGN. From this asymmetry, we constrain the average physical magnetic field in the proto-ICM to a lower limit of 0.4 $μ$G. These results confirm a magnetised proto-ICM at z = 1.72, proving early field amplification during cluster assembly.

</details>


### [30] [Complex yet Hermitian: Gaussian covariance of cross-correlation and multi-tracer power spectra](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12551)
*Federico Montano,Stefano Camera,Emiliano Sefusatti,Mohamed Yousry Elkhashab*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文推广了多示踪器功率谱测量的高斯协方差理论结果，提出适用于实数（偶宇称）和复数（偶、奇宇称）功率谱的一般表达式，并通过高斯蒙特卡洛模拟验证其准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前及未来巡天数据对大尺度结构信号的约束精度不断提高，亟需精确建模聚类可观测量的协方差；模拟方法计算成本高，且多示踪器分析与宇称奇信号日益重要，因此需发展高效解析协方差模型。

Method: 推广已有高斯协方差理论，构建适用于通用加权估计器、勒让德多极矩及二维功率谱的统一解析表达式，并分析协方差矩阵的厄米特性（尤其虚部）。

Result: 推导出适用于实数和复数功率谱的通用高斯协方差表达式；成功复现已知极限情形；通过高斯蒙特卡洛模拟验证预测精度；揭示协方差虚部的厄米结构。

Conclusion: 所提出的通用协方差框架为多示踪器和宇称奇两体统计分析提供了坚实的理论基础，有助于提升宇宙学参数约束精度并降低计算开销。

Abstract: Accurate modelling of the covariance of clustering observables is essential to fully exploit current and future survey data, which is expected to constrain large-scale clustering signals with unprecedented precision. Computational costs of simulation-based estimates motivate analytical approaches, especially in light of the growing interest towards multi-tracer analyses and parity-odd signatures in two-point statistics, which respectively mitigate cosmic variance and probe relativistic projection effects on cosmological scales. In this work, we generalise previous theoretical results for the Gaussian covariance of multi-tracer power spectrum measurements, providing a general expression applicable to both real (even-parity) and complex (both even- and odd-parity) power spectra. We focus on a generic weighted estimator at first, and then showcase how our general formalism applies to Legendre power spectrum multipoles and two-dimensional power spectrum, recovering known limits in appropriate cases. We validate our predictions against Gaussian Monte Carlo simulations and investigate the structure of the covariance matrix, including the Hermitian properties of its imaginary part.

### [31] [Galaxy formation in modified gravity -- II. galaxy halo connection and assembly bias](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12565)
*Michael Collier,Sownak Bose,Baojiu Li*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文利用f(R)引力下的模拟数据研究了星系-晕关联在修正引力模型中的表现，发现标准HOD模型在忽略装配偏差时会低估星系聚集强度，而引入环境密度作为次级变量可显著减小该偏差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大型星系巡天（如DESI、Euclid）旨在通过大尺度结构精确测定宇宙学参数，但受限于对星系-晕关联（尤其在修正引力模型中）理解不足，特别是装配偏差（AB）的影响。

Method: 基于前沿的修正引力（f(R)）流体动力学模拟，构建匹配Stage-IV巡天规格的发射线星系（ELG）和亮红星系（LRG）模拟样本，并分析 halo occupation distribution (HOD) 模型及其扩展形式（加入环境密度作为次级变量）对装配偏差的刻画能力。

Result: 在ΛCDM中忽略装配偏差时，标准HOD模型在z≲1时低估星系聚集强度10–20%；在f(R)引力中偏差更复杂；引入环境密度作为HOD次变量后，z≲0.5时装配偏差降至2–3%。

Conclusion: 环境密度是缓解装配偏差、提升修正引力模型下星系-晕建模精度的有效物理参数，为未来用大尺度结构检验非标准宇宙学模型提供了可靠起点。

Abstract: Modern surveys such as DESI and \textit{Euclid}, which collect data for hundreds of millions of galaxies to map the large-scale structure (LSS) of the Universe, hold the key to determining the cosmological parameters and testing new physics. This ambition, however, is limited by uncertainties in the galaxy-halo connection: the link between observed galaxies and the underlying, unobservable matter field, by accounting for effects such as galaxy bias and assembly bias (AB). These are particularly poorly-understood for modified gravity (MG) models, which are popular alternatives to the cosmological constant to explain accelerated expansion. We approach this problem using mock emission line galaxy (ELG) and luminous red galaxy (LRG) catalogues in $f(R)$ gravity matching the specifications of ongoing Stage-IV galaxy surveys, generated from state-of-the-art MG hydrodynamical simulations. While the interplay between MG -- especially the chameleon screening mechanism -- and galaxy formation leaves complicated imprints in the galaxy-halo connection, a simple physical picture emerges in which halo and galaxy formation are enhanced for progressively more massive haloes over time. We confirm that the basic galaxy-halo connection model, the halo occupation distribution (HOD), in which galaxy occupation is determined solely by halo mass, underestimates galaxy clustering strength in $Λ$CDM by $10$--$20\%$ at $z\lesssim1$ when neglecting AB, and demonstrate that MG introduces further complexity. Extending this model with a suitably-chosen environment density as a secondary HOD variable reduces the AB effect in all models to $2$--$3\%$ for $z\lesssim0.5$. This provides a well-motivated starting point for further works on minimising the impact of AB when testing non-standard cosmological models with LSS.

### [32] [Weak Lensing Spectrotomography: A1767 and A2065](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12613)
*Jubee Sohn,Ian P. Dell'Antonio,Margaret J. Geller*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文首次利用存档的Subaru/HSC成像数据，结合光谱红移，对星系团A1767和A2065开展光谱断层弱引力透镜测量（spectrotomography），获得3.1σ和3.5σ的剪切信号探测，并验证其与动力学质量一致；同时指出亮背景星系可能引入系统误差，为未来Euclid和LSST等巡天中的无偏星系团质量测量和几何宇宙学检验奠定基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 克服传统光度红移带来的系统误差，实现更干净、无偏的星系团弱透镜质量测量，并探索其在几何宇宙学检验中的潜力。

Method: 采用光谱断层弱透镜（spectrotomography）方法，仅使用本文新报告的具有光谱红移的背景星系，结合Subaru/HSC成像数据，分离星系团成员与背景源。

Result: 在A1767和A2065中分别以3.1σ和3.5σ置信度探测到断层剪切信号，幅度与动力学质量一致且随源红移合理变化；但对比A2029发现亮背景星系可能引入细微系统误差。

Conclusion: 首次基于HSC存档数据实现spectrotomography，三项成功探测（A1767/A2029/A2065）验证该技术可行性，为未来大样本无偏星系团质量测量及独立几何宇宙学检验铺平道路。

Abstract: We describe spectroscopic tomographic weak lensing measurements (spectrotomography) for two rich clusters of galaxies, A1767 and A2065, based on extensive spectroscopy and Subaru/Hyper Suprime-Cam (HSC) imaging. These detections represent the first use of spectrotomography based on archival Subaru/HSC imaging. The measurements depend only on galaxies with spectroscopic redshifts reported here. The approach cleanly separates cluster members from the background and suppresses systematics that may be introduced by the use of photometric background redshifts. We detect the tomographic shear signals at $3.1σ$ (A1767) and $3.5σ$ (A2065). The shear signal amplitudes are consistent with the cluster dynamical (caustic) masses and they scale appropriately with source redshift. However, comparison with the first spectrophotometric detection of A2029 based on DECam imaging reveals some subtle potential systematic issues in deriving the shear signal for the relatively bright background galaxies used in the analysis. These issues may be important for understanding future more extensive applications of spectrotomography based on further Subaru imaging, as well as Euclid and LSST data. The total of three spectrophotometric detections (A1767, A2029, and A2065) sets the stage for broader application of the technique for unbiased cluster weak lensing mass determinations and potentially for a geometric cosmological test that is independent of other methods.

### [33] [Identification of Lensed Gravitational-Wave Beat Patterns by LISA](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12792)
*Hengyu Wu,Tonghua Liu,Kai Liao*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文研究了大质量黑洞双星系统在强引力透镜作用下产生的多个引力波图像及其叠加形成的拍频模式，提出了一种基于拍频模板的贝叶斯参数估计方法，并评估了LISA探测中可识别拍频事件的发生率约为7%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 利用LISA长期观测能力，探索强引力透镜对大质量黑洞双星引力波信号的影响，特别是重叠 inspiral 阶段产生的拍频模式这一新观测特征。

Method: 采用奇异等温球透镜模型构建双像拍频波形；仅在首像并合前的重叠旋进阶段计算波形失配以提取拍频；基于HS-nod-SN强透镜种群模拟统计可识别拍频事件，并用拍频模板进行贝叶斯参数估计。

Result: 在196个可探测双像透镜事件中，92个满足时间重叠条件，14个满足拍频可识别标准（占比约7%）；贝叶斯推断能有效恢复透镜时间延迟和放大率参数。

Conclusion: 强透镜产生的拍频模式是LISA可观测的一类独特且可区分的信号，为LISA波段强引力透镜提供了新的观测标识。

Abstract: Strong lensing of massive black hole binaries can produce multiple gravitational-wave images with different magnifications and arrival times. LISA signals remain in band for months to years, allowing multiple lensed images to overlap during the inspiral stage and generate beat patterns. A singular isothermal sphere lens model is adopted to describe the lensing configuration, and two-image beat waveforms are constructed from massive black hole binary signals. To isolate the beat pattern itself, waveform mismatch is evaluated only during the overlapping inspiral stage before the coalescence of the first image, excluding contributions from the delayed merger peak of the second image. Using the HS-nod-SN (B+20) strong-lensing population, the occurrence rate of identifiable beat events is estimated, and Bayesian parameter estimation is performed with a beat template. Beat patterns are most readily identified when the lensing time delay is short and the delayed image has a relatively large magnification. Among 196 detectable two-image lensed events, 92 satisfy the temporal-overlap condition and 14 satisfy the beat-identification criterion, corresponding to an identifiable beat fraction of about 7\%. Posterior inference shows that the beat template can recover the lensing time delay and magnification parameters for a representative beat event. These results indicate that lensed beat patterns constitute a distinguishable subset of strongly lensed LISA events and provide a unique observational signature of strong lensing in the LISA band.
